about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> Interface management is
  the primary focus and students learned various approaches to conduct interface management
  for system integration.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Olivier de Weck</p>

  <span m='1773440'>exchanging</span> <span m='1774070'>the</span> <span m='1774160'>heat,</span>

  </p><p><span m='1775960'>So a</span> <span m='1776290'>heat</span> <span m='1776500'>exchanger</span>
  <span m='1777010'>is</span> <span m='1777130'>interesting</span> <span m='1777700'>because</span>
  <span m='1778960'>what</span> <span m='1779170'>kind</span> <span m='1779410'>of</span>
  <span m='1779470'>flows</span> <span m='1779940'>happen</span> <span m='1780350'>in</span>
  <span m='1780520'>a</span> <span m='1780580'>heat</span> <span m='1780760'>exchanger</span>
  <span m='1784270'>of</span> <span m='1784440'>the</span> <span m='1784560'>flows</span>
  <span m='1784920'>we've</span> <span m='1785070'>discussed</span> <span m='1785460'>so</span>
  <span m='1785640'>far?</span> <span m='1788160'>Energy</span> <span m='1789300'>and</span>
  <span m='1789630'>mass</span> <span m='1789960'>flow,</span> <span m='1790290'>right?</span>
  <span m='1790680'>So</span> <span m='1790890'>the</span> <span m='1791010'>two</span>
  <span m='1791250'>of</span> <span m='1791340'>them</span> <span m='1791520'>happen</span>

  <span m='1796770'>happen</span> <span m='1797100'>as</span> <span m='1797220'>well.</span>
  <span m='1797980'>So</span> <span m='1798030'>these</span> <span m='1798180'>two</span>
